            "url": "https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/57138546",

            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/c1302697e06e8016d3b979dd723e311a", 
            "upvote": 2, 
            "title": "C语言学习之结构体", 
            "content": "<h2>前言</h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-be797b207ffa41dba574c3b16337475d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"449\" data-rawheight=\"250\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"449\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-be797b207ffa41dba574c3b16337475d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;449&#39; height=&#39;250&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"449\" data-rawheight=\"250\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"449\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-be797b207ffa41dba574c3b16337475d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-be797b207ffa41dba574c3b16337475d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>一直以来，C语言的学习都在入门阶段，只用到数组、函数、循环、选择、位运算这些基本的知识，较少用到指针、预处理、结构体、枚举类型、文件操作等这些C语言的精髓内容，现在想想真不敢说自己<b>熟练掌握C语言的使用</b>，所以最近几篇文章是关于这些内容的，一方面是巩固自己的C语言编程能力，另一方面也为以后学习C++做准备。</p><h2>什么是结构体</h2><p>C语言的结构体实际上就是一种特殊的数据类型，只不过这种数据类型包括了很多个基本类型的数据，如int、float、char等等，如在开发学生成绩管理系统时，有学号、姓名、院系、班级、年龄、各个科目、各个科目对应的成绩等，不使用结构体我们需要定义许多的变量，而使用结构体可以大大简化程序的设计，</p><h2>结构体类型的定义</h2><p>结构体的定义格式为：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct 结构体名称\n{\n    结构体所包含的成员变量；\n}</code></pre></div><p>与C++不同的是，C语言的结构体只能包括成员变量，不能包含成员函数，但可以定义函数指针指向一个函数。</p><p>定义一个名为student的结构体类型，包含id、name、score这3个成员变量。</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct student\n{\n    int id;\n    char *name;\n    float score;\n};</code></pre></div><p>定义两个student的结构体变量：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct student lucy, jack;</code></pre></div><p>当然，也可以在定义结构体的同时定义结构体变量：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct student\n{\n    int id;\n    char *name;\n    float score;\n}lucy, jack;</code></pre></div><p>即把变量名放在定义结构体的最后即可。</p><p>如果只需要定义lucy、jack两个结构体变量，后面其他地方都不需要再定义新的结构体变量，那么结构体名可以省略，不建议使用这种方式：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct \n{\n    int id;\n    char *name;\n    float score;\n}lucy, jack;</code></pre></div><p>这种写法看起来是稍微简单了一些，但后面无法再定义新的结构体变量。</p><h2>结构体变量在内存中的存储</h2><p>理论上和数组元素的存储非常类似，结构体变量的存储也是连续存储的，但在实际的编译器实现过程中，各个成员变量之间可能会存在缝隙。</p><h2>结构体变量</h2><p>【示例】：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &#34;stdio.h&#34;\n#include &#34;stdlib.h&#34;\n\nstruct student\n{\n    int id;\n    char *name;\n    float score;\n};\n\nstruct student jack;\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    //成员的赋值\n    jack.id = 1234;\n    jack.name = &#34;jack&#34;;\n    jack.score = 89.5;\n\n    printf(&#34;%s id: %d, score: %.1f \\r\\n&#34;, jack.name, jack.id, jack.score);\n\n    return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p>【输出结果】：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">jack id: 1234, score: 89.5</code></pre></div><p>当然，也可以在定义的时候整体赋值：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct student lucy, jack = {1233, &#34;jack&#34;, 92.6};</code></pre></div><p>但不可以在定义之后，单独整体赋值；</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct student lucy;\nlucy = {1233, &#34;lucy&#34;, 92.6};</code></pre></div><p>这种整体赋值不允许，会报错。</p><h2>结构体数组</h2><p>当然也允许定义结构体数组：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct student cls[5];</code></pre></div><p>定义的数组可以不指定数组大小。</p><p>【示例】：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &#34;stdio.h&#34;\n#include &#34;stdlib.h&#34;\n\nstruct student\n{\n    int id;\n    char *name;\n    float score;\n};\n//定义的同时整体赋值\nstruct student cls[5] =     //也可以不给出数据大小: cls[]\n{\n    {1001, &#34;Li Lei&#34;, 88.4},\n    {1002, &#34;Zhang Wei&#34;, 79.3},\n    {1003, &#34;Wang Ming&#34;, 70.8},\n    {1004,&#34;Zhao Yang&#34;, 80.5},\n    {1005,&#34;Li Liang&#34;, 89.5}\n};\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    int i;\n    int num_80 = 0; //分数大于80的人数\n    float average = 0, sum = 0;     //平均分和总和\n\n    for(i = 0; i &lt; 5; i++)\n    {\n        sum += cls[i].score;\n        if(cls[i].score &gt; 80)\n            num_80++;\n    }\n    average = sum / 5.0;\n\n    printf(&#34;分数大于80的人数：%d，总平均分：%.1f&#34;, num_80, average);  \n    return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p>【输出结果】：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">分数大于80的人数：3，总平均分：81.7</code></pre></div><h2>结构体指针变量</h2><p>定义格式为：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">struct student *p;</code></pre></div><p>【示例一】：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &#34;stdio.h&#34;\n#include &#34;stdlib.h&#34;\n\nstruct student\n{\n    int id;\n    char *name;\n    float score;\n};\n//定义的同时整体赋值\nstruct student *pstu, stu = {1234, &#34;lucy&#34;, 90.4};\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    pstu = &amp;stu;        //*pstu 等同于 stu\n\n    printf(&#34;id: %d, name: %s, score: %.1f \\n&#34;, stu.id, stu.name, stu.score);\n    printf(&#34;id: %d, name: %s, score: %.1f \\n&#34;, (*pstu).id, (*pstu).name, (*pstu).score);\n    printf(&#34;id: %d, name: %s, score: %.1f \\n&#34;, pstu-&gt;id, pstu-&gt;name, pstu-&gt;score);  //指针变量引用成员变量\n\n    return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p>【输出结果】：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">id: 1234, name: lucy, score: 90.4\nid: 1234, name: lucy, score: 90.4\nid: 1234, name: lucy, score: 90.4</code></pre></div><p>【示例二】</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &#34;stdio.h&#34;\n#include &#34;stdlib.h&#34;\n\nstruct student\n{\n    int id;\n    char *name;\n    float score;\n};\n\nstruct student *ps;\nstruct student cls[] =\n{\n    {1001, &#34;Li Lei&#34;, 88.4},\n    {1002, &#34;Zhang Wei&#34;, 79.3},\n    {1003, &#34;Wang Ming&#34;, 70.8},\n    {1004,&#34;Zhao Yang&#34;, 80.5},\n    {1005,&#34;Li Liang&#34;, 89.5}\n};\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    int len = sizeof(cls) / sizeof(struct student);    //求数组长度\n    printf(&#34;id \\t name \\t score \\n&#34;);\n\n    for(ps = cls; ps &lt; cls + len; ps++)\n    {\n        printf(&#34;%d \\t %s \\t %.1f \\n&#34;, ps-&gt;id, ps-&gt;name, ps-&gt;score);\n    }\n    return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p>【输出结果】：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">id       name    score\n1001     Li Lei          88.4\n1002     Zhang Wei       79.3\n1003     Wang Ming       70.8\n1004     Zhao Yang       80.5\n1005     Li Liang        89.5</code></pre></div><hr/><p>参考资料：</p><ul><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//c.biancheng.net/c/100/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">C语言结构体详解</a></li></ul><p>Jlink使用技巧系列文章：</p><ul><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/2019/01/17/Jlink-merge/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Jlink使用技巧之合并烧写文件</a></li><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/2019/01/12/Jlink-SPI-Flash/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Jlink使用技巧之烧写SPI Flash存储</a></li><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/2019/01/09/Jlink-UART/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Jlink使用技巧之虚拟串口功能</a></li><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/2019/01/06/Jlink-ReadBack-Hex/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Jlink使用技巧之读取STM32内部的程序</a></li><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/2018/10/17/JScope/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Jlink使用技巧之J-Scope虚拟示波器功能</a></li><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/2019/01/05/Jlink-Download-Hex/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Jlink使用技巧之单独下载HEX文件到单片机</a></li></ul><hr/><p>欢迎大家关注我的<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/\" class=\" wrap external\"             "content": "<p>下面两个简单的程序哪个更规范、可读性更高呢？</p><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d6e987cfbc8d748b65c9546910ad61c4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"1075\" data-rawheight=\"656\" width=\"1075\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d6e987cfbc8d748b65c9546910ad61c4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d6e987cfbc8d748b65c9546910ad61c4_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p>\n显然是右侧的，合理缩进、美观、可读性高，是规范的代码风格。当我们使用Kei编写程序时，往往不注意代码的风格，那么有没有一种工具能让代码自动调整为标准格式呢？答案是肯定的，那就是Astyle插件，</p><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><p><b>关于</b><b>AStyle </b></p><blockquote>\nAStyle 是Artistic\nStyle的简称，是一个开源的源代码格式化工具，可以对C，C++，C#以及Java等编程语言的源代码进行缩进、格式化、美化，该插件基于\nArtistic Style 开发，可在\nEclipse CDT 环境中使用。</blockquote><p><b>准备：</b></p><p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//nbct01.baidupcs.com/file/6a78a4942ea24f8da656035c96387c52%3Fbkt%3Dp3-14006a78a4942ea24f8da656035c96387c52d475a5f400000005984e%26fid%3D2233616269-250528-959669243202148%26time%3D1476680247%26sign%3DFDTAXGERLBH-DCb740ccc5511e5e8fedcff06b081203-QRu7aJShaGiOS4YNcQfq44S/ue0%3D%26to%3Dnbhb%26fm%3DNin%2CB%2CU%2Cnc%26sta_dx%3D366670%26sta_cs%3D7%26sta_ft%3Dzip%26sta_ct%3D0%26sta_mt%3D0%26fm2%3DNingbo%2CB%2CU%2Cnc%26newver%3D1%26newfm%3D1%26secfm%3D1%26flow_ver%3D3%26pkey%3D14006a78a4942ea24f8da656035c96387c52d475a5f400000005984e%26sl%3D83492943%26expires%3D8h%26rt%3Dpr%26r%3D464360919%26mlogid%3D6738440740533384249%26vuk%3D2233616269%26vbdid%3D562512071%26fin%3DAStyle_2.02.1_windows.zip%26fn%3DAStyle_2.02.1_windows.zip%26slt%3Dpm%26uta%3D0%26rtype%3D1%26iv%3D0%26isw%3D0%26dp-logid%3D6738440740533384249%26dp-callid%3D0.1.1%26csl%3D293%26csign%3DdGfQSWQraNkIZ21niaBwpacf34o%3D\" 软件，选择<b>Tools</b>菜单下的<b>Customize\nTools Menu</b>选项。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4d940fe13a0150e7573bc38bdebb54b7_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"500\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3a58399eaf6d5f1630c7ca13c6a4693b_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>四、</b>新建插件，命名<b>AStyle\nCurrent File</b>（可以任意名字），<br/></p><p><b>Command</b>：输入<b>AStyle.exe</b>文件的路径，或点击到Keil\\AStyle\\bin目录下选择AStyle.exe。</p><p><b>Arguments:</b>输入<b>-p\n!E</b>，其中<b>!E</b>表示将当前代码格式化，<b>-p</b> 表示在操作符两边添加空格，注意<b>-p</b>与<b>!E</b>之间有个空格，<b>p</b>为小写字母。</p><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fdf8f18989d5a0a16a0904937cf331e3_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fdf8f18989d5a0a16a0904937cf331e3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fdf8f18989d5a0a16a0904937cf331e3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fdf8f18989d5a0a16a0904937cf331e3_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>五、</b>插件安装好了，应该怎么使用呢?</p><p>\n程序编写完成后，单击<b>Tools</b>菜单下的<b>AStyle\nCurrent File</b></p><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a322b65b9e5a98d55c595b0a4b3fe107_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2edc9453782e72ce3f13a444b425ae3e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2edc9453782e72ce3f13a444b425ae3e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2edc9453782e72ce3f13a444b425ae3e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2edc9453782e72ce3f13a444b425ae3e_b.png\"/></figure><br/><br/><p><b>Build\nOutput </b>窗口显示已经格式化当前C文件，运行后，文件就是标准的C代码格式了，是不是很神奇呢？</p><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-77a964792f0fef6556958c85cf32f533_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"485\" data-rawheight=\"613\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"485\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-77a964792f0fef6556958c85cf32f533_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;485&#39; height=&#39;613&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"485\" data-rawheight=\"613\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"485\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-77a964792f0fef6556958c85cf32f533_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-77a964792f0fef6556958c85cf32f533_b.png\"/></figure><br/><br/><p><b>六、</b>插件添加成功后，还可以为这个插件自定义的一个快捷键，以方便我们的操作：</p><p><b>1</b><b>．选择</b><b>Edit</b><b>菜单下的</b><b>Configuration</b><b>选项。</b></p><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7eeab81dc9f941621351310e17bb4344_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"828\" data-rawheight=\"629\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"828\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7eeab81dc9f941621351310e17bb4344_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;828&#39; height=&#39;629&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"828\" data-rawheight=\"629\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"828\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7eeab81dc9f941621351310e17bb4344_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7eeab81dc9f941621351310e17bb4344_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>2.</b><b>选择</b><b>ShortcutKeys</b><b>选项卡下的</b><b>Tools</b><b>：</b><b>AStyleCurrent\nFile </b><b>点击</b><b>Create\nShortcut</b><b>。</b></p><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e726e7af096568bcff815fd220af4146_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"1044\" data-rawheight=\"631\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1044\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e726e7af096568bcff815fd220af4146_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1044&#39; height=&#39;631&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"1044\" data-rawheight=\"631\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1044\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e726e7af096568bcff815fd220af4146_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e726e7af096568bcff815fd220af4146_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>3.</b><b>在弹出的窗口，按下要设置的快捷键，笔者是设置为</b><b>Ctrl+Shift+A</b><b>，点击</b><b>OK</b><b>确定。</b></p><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18377c9dae520cf6b18756a2f9f3ec49_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"838\" data-rawheight=\"647\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"838\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18377c9dae520cf6b18756a2f9f3ec49_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;838&#39; height=&#39;647&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"838\" data-rawheight=\"647\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"838\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18377c9dae520cf6b18756a2f9f3ec49_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-18377c9dae520cf6b18756a2f9f3ec49_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>4.</b><b>这样格式化文件的快捷键就设置好了，快试试好不好用吧！是不是比用鼠标更方便了呢！</b></p><br/><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5f14f07d5af5aac5e95c34656862569c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5f14f07d5af5aac5e95c34656862569c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;500&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5f14f07d5af5aac5e95c34656862569c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5f14f07d5af5aac5e95c34656862569c_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p>设置的默认格式为ANSI格式，另外还可以设置为其他的代码格式，如kr或linux或gnu等其他格式，只需要<b>Argument</b>项命令符前面加上：<b>--style= 某格式</b></p><p>\n如设置为kr代码格式:</p><p><b>Argument：--style=kr-p\n!E </b></p><br/><p>\n下图是kr格式和ansi格式，可以看出两种格式非常接近。<figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f749e2484f74dacf084de01db9ebec2_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"1181\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1181\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f749e2484f74dacf084de01db9ebec2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1181&#39; height=&#39;500&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"1181\" data-rawheight=\"500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1181\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f749e2484f74dacf084de01db9ebec2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f749e2484f74dacf084de01db9ebec2_b.png\"/></figure></p><p><b>附录：</b></p><p><b>AStyle</b><b>常用命令符：</b></p><p><b>(1)-f</b></p><p>\n在两行不相关的代码之间插入空行，如import和public\nclass之间、public\nclass和成员之间等；</p><p><b>(2)-p</b></p><p>\n在操作符两边插入空格，如=、+、-等。</p><p>如：inta=10*60;</p><p>处理后变成int a = 10 * 60;</p><p><b>(3)-P</b></p><p>\n在括号两边插入空格。另，-d只在括号外面插入空格，-D只在里面插入。</p><p>如：MessageBox.Show(&#34;aaa&#34;);</p><p>处理后变成MessageBox.Show ( &#34;aaa&#34; );</p><p><b>(4)-U</b></p><p>移除括号两边不必要的空格。</p><p>如：MessageBox.Show( &#34;aaa&#34; );</p><p>处理后变成MessageBox.Show (&#34;aaa&#34;);</p><p><b>(5)-V</b></p><p>将Tab替换为空格。</p><p>参考：</p><p>​<b><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.keil.com/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Keil µVision4 User&#39;s\nGuide</a></b></p><p><b><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//baike.baidu.com/link%3Furl%3DOAFHbDwFct3QJFsseUvBi_5jBiNZF17HHQhd2ORD2BcSepwVojA2Vadwo803I7zmQE2ftUPklI0ri8Gs0_qEEK\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">AStyle_百度百科</a></b></p><p><b><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//AStyle.sourceforge.net/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">AStyle使用帮助</a></b></p>",

            "title": "C标准库string.h中几个常用函数的使用详解", 
            "content": "<h2>strlen</h2><p>计算字符串长度</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-c\"><span class=\"n\">size_t</span> <span class=\"n\">strlen</span><span class=\"p\">(</span><span class=\"k\">const</span> <span class=\"kt\">char</span> <span class=\"o\">*</span><span class=\"n\">str</span><span class=\"p\">)</span></code></pre></div><p>计算字符串 str 的长度，直到空结束字符，但不包括空结束字符。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Strlen(const char *str)\n{\n    assert(str);\n    int len = 0;\n    while ((*str++) != &#39;\\0&#39;)len++;\n    return len;\n}</code></pre></div><h2>strcpy</h2><p>字符串复制</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *strcpy(char *dest, const char *src)</code></pre></div><p>把 src 所指向的字符串复制到 dest。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *Strcpy(char *dst, const char *src)\n{\n    assert(dst &amp;&amp; src);\n    char *tmp = dst;\n    while ((*dst++ = *src++) != &#39;\\0&#39;);\n    return tmp;\n}</code></pre></div><h2>strncpy</h2><p>复制连续的n个字符</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *strncpy(char *dest, const char *src, size_t n)</code></pre></div><p>把 src 所指向的字符串复制到 dest，最多复制 n 个字符。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *Strncpy(char *dst, const char *src, int len)\n{\n    assert(dst&amp;&amp;src);\n    char *tmp = dst;\n    int offset = 0;\n    if (len &gt; strlen(src))\n    {\n        offset = len - strlen(src);\n        len = strlen(src);\n    }\n    while (len--)\n    {\n        *dst++ = *src++;\n    }\n    while (offset--)\n    {\n        *dst++ = &#39;\\0&#39;;\n    }\n    return tmp;\n}</code></pre></div><h2>strcat</h2><p>把一个字符串连接到另一个字符串后面</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *strcat(char *dest, const char *src)</code></pre></div><p>把 src 所指向的字符串追加到 dest 所指向的字符串的结尾。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *Strcat(char *dst, const char* src)\n{\n    assert(dst &amp;&amp; src);\n    char *tmp = dst;\n    while (*dst++);\n    dst--;\n    while (*dst++ = *src++);\n    return tmp;\n}</code></pre></div><h2>strncat</h2><p>把连续的n个字符连接到另一个字符串后面</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *strncat(char *dest, const char *src, size_t n)</code></pre></div><p>把 src 所指向的字符串追加到 dest 所指向的字符串的结尾，直到 n 字符长度为止。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *Strncat(char *dst, const char* src, int len)\n{\n    assert(dst &amp;&amp; src);\n    char *tmp = dst;\n    while (*dst++);\n    dst--;\n    while (len--)\n    {\n        *dst++ = *src++;\n    }\n    *dst = &#39;\\0&#39;;\n    return tmp;\n}</code></pre></div><p>示例：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\n#include &lt;string.h&gt;\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    char str0[20] = &#34;Test:&#34;;\n    char str1[20] = &#34;Welcome9999&#34;;\n    char str2[20] = &#34; To &#34;;\n    char str3[20] = &#34;0123Beijing55&#34;;\n    char tmp[100];\n\n    strcpy(tmp, str0);\n    puts(tmp);      //Test:\n\n    strncpy(tmp, str1, 7);  //取st1前7个字符\n    puts(tmp);      //Welcome\n\n    strcat(tmp, str2);      //连接str2\n    puts(tmp);\n\n    strncat(tmp, str3 + 4, 7);  //取str3+4之后的7个字符\n    puts(tmp);\n\n    return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p>输出结果：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-74160caabb9b2360a128a479c48ccba1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1247\" data-rawheight=\"627\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1247\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-74160caabb9b2360a128a479c48ccba1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1247&#39; height=&#39;627&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1247\" data-rawheight=\"627\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1247\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-74160caabb9b2360a128a479c48ccba1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-74160caabb9b2360a128a479c48ccba1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>strchr</h2><p>查找某字符在字符串中首次出现的位置指针，如果不存在则返回NULL</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *strchr(const char *str, int c)</code></pre></div><p>在参数 str 所指向的字符串中搜索第一次出现字符 c（一个无符号字符）的位置。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char* My_strchr(char *s, char c)\n{\n    while(*s != &#39;\\0&#39; &amp;&amp; *s != c)\n    {\n        ++s;\n    }\n    return *s==c ? s : NULL;\n}</code></pre></div><p>示例：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &lt;string.h&gt;\n#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\nint main(void)\n{\n    char string[20] = &#34;This is a string&#34;;\n    char *ptr1, *ptr2;\n    char c1 = &#39;r&#39;, c2 = &#39;b&#39;;\n\n    ptr1 = strchr(string, c1);\n    ptr2 = strchr(string, c2);\n\n    if(ptr1)\n        printf(&#34;字符1:%c 的位置是: %s \\n&#34;,c1,ptr1);\n    else\n        printf(&#34;字符1:%c 未找到 \\n&#34;, c1);\n\n    if(ptr2)\n        printf(&#34;字符2:%c 的位置是: %s \\n&#34;,c2,ptr2);\n    else\n        printf(&#34;字符2:%c 未找到 \\n&#34;, c2);\n\n    return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p>输出结果：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4bcc3a0ecd023ad54d9d6204135627c0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1187\" data-rawheight=\"452\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1187\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4bcc3a0ecd023ad54d9d6204135627c0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1187&#39; height=&#39;452&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1187\" data-rawheight=\"452\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1187\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4bcc3a0ecd023ad54d9d6204135627c0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4bcc3a0ecd023ad54d9d6204135627c0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>strcmp</h2><p>字符串比较</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int strcmp(const char *str1, const char *str2)</code></pre></div><p>把 str1 所指向的字符串和 str2 所指向的字符串进行比较。</p><p>设这两个字符串为str1，str2， 若str1=str2，则返回零； 若str1str2，则返回正数。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Strcmp(char const *s1, char const *s2)\n{\n    assert(s1&amp;&amp;s2);\n    while (*s1 == *s2 &amp;&amp; *s1 != &#39;\\0&#39; &amp;&amp; *s2 != &#39;\\0&#39;)\n    {\n        s1++;\n        s2++;\n    }\n    if (*s1 == *s2)\n    {\n        return 0;\n    }\n    else if (*s1 &gt; *s2)\n    {\n        return 1;\n    }\n    return -1;\n}</code></pre></div><p>示例：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &lt;string.h&gt;\n#include &lt;stdio.h&gt;\nint main(void)\n{\n    char str1[20] = &#34;abc&#34;;\n    char str2[20] = &#34;abc&#34;;\n    char str3[20] = &#34;bbc&#34;;\n\n    int r1, r2, r3;\n\n    r1 = strcmp(str1, str2);\n    r2 = strcmp(str1, str3);\n    r3 = strcmp(str3, str1);\n\n    printf(&#34;r1 = %d, r2 = %d, r3 = %d \\n&#34;, r1, r2, r3);\n\n    return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p>输出结果：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-59f687c90ebbee8951ca21a1dcdb4912_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1243\" data-rawheight=\"467\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1243\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-59f687c90ebbee8951ca21a1dcdb4912_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1243&#39; height=&#39;467&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1243\" data-rawheight=\"467\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1243\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-59f687c90ebbee8951ca21a1dcdb4912_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-59f687c90ebbee8951ca21a1dcdb4912_b.jpg\"/></figure><h2>strstr</h2><p>字符串查找</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *strstr(const char *haystack, const char *needle)</code></pre></div><p>在字符串 haystack 中查找第一次出现字符串 needle（不包含空结束字符）的位置。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">char *Strstr(char const *s1, char const *s2)\n{\n    assert(s1&amp;&amp;s2);\n    const char *ps1, *ps2;\n    ps1 = s1;\n    ps2 = s2;\n    while (*ps1)\n    {\n        const char *tmp = ps1;\n        while (*tmp++ == *ps2++);\n        if (*ps2 == &#39;\\0&#39;)\n        {\n            return (char*)ps1;\n        }\n        ps2 = s2;\n        ps1++;\n    }\n    return NULL;\n}</code></pre></div><h2>strncmp</h2><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int strncmp(const char *str1, const char *str2, size_t n)</code></pre></div><p>把 str1 和 str2 进行比较，最多比较前 n 个字节。</p><p>函数实现：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Strncmp(char const *s1, char const *s2, int len)\n{\n    assert(s1&amp;&amp;s2);\n    while (len-- &amp;&amp; *s1 == *s2 &amp;&amp; *s1 != &#39;\\0&#39; &amp;&amp; *s2 != &#39;\\0&#39;)\n    {\n        s1++;\n        s2++;\n    }\n    return *s1 - *s2;\n}</code></pre></div><h2>memcpy</h2><p>内存复制</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">void *memcpy(void *dest, const void *src, size_t n)</code></pre></div><p>从 src 复制 n 个字符到 dest。</p><p>函数实现</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">void *Memcpy(char *dst, char const *src, int len)\n{\n    assert(dst &amp;&amp; src);\n    char *tmp = dst;\n    const char *s = src;\n    while (len--)\n    {\n        *dst++ = *src;\n    }\n    return tmp;\n}</code></pre></div><hr/><p>Jlink使用技巧系列文章：</p><ul><li><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//www.wangchaochao.top/2019/01/17/Jlink-merge/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\"             "url": "https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/55565716", 
            "userName": "王超", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/c1302697e06e8016d3b979dd723e311a", 
            "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "一键自动格式化你的代码", 
            "content": "<h2>AStyle简介</h2><p>AStyle，即Artistic Style，是一个可用于C, C++, C++/CLI, Objective‑C, C# 和Java编程语言格式化和美化的工具。我们在使用编辑器的缩进（TAB）功能时，由于不同编辑器的差别，有的插入的是制表符，有的是2个空格，有的是4个空格。这样如果别人用另一个编辑器来阅读程序时，可能会由于缩进的不同，导致阅读效果一团糟。为了解决这个问题，使用C++开发了一个插件，它可以自动重新缩进，并手动指定空格的数量，自动格式化源文件。它是可以通过命令行使用，也可以作为插件，在其他IDE中使用。</p><h2>基本使用</h2><p>下载完成后，解压，然后在环境变量PATH，添加AStyle.exe的路径。</p><p>基本命令行格式：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">astyle [参数] [文件路径]</code></pre></div><p>如在我的电脑E盘下有一个文件main.c，现在是这样的，可以看出很不规范，多个语句写在同一行，没有合理缩进，运算符两边没有空格等等。</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &#34;sys.h&#34;\n#include &#34;delay.h&#34;\n#include &#34;usart.h&#34;\n#include &#34;led.h&#34;\n\nint main(void)\n{\ndelay_init();       //延时函数初始化\nLED_Init();         //初始化与LED连接的硬件接口\nwhile(1)\n{\nLED0=0;LED1=1;\ndelay_ms(300);  //延时300ms\nLED0= 1;LED1 =0;\ndelay_ms(300);  //延时300ms\n}\n}</code></pre></div><p>打开CMD命令窗口，输入以下命令：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">AStyle --style=ansi E:\\main.c</code></pre></div><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-62d75b5214a3d829505011034df9715e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"496\" data-rawheight=\"197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"496\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-62d75b5214a3d829505011034df9715e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;496&#39; height=&#39;197&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"496\" data-rawheight=\"197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"496\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-62d75b5214a3d829505011034df9715e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-62d75b5214a3d829505011034df9715e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>回车执行命令，然后再打开main.c查看，变成了这样：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">#include &#34;sys.h&#34;\n#include &#34;delay.h&#34;\n#include &#34;usart.h&#34;\n#include &#34;led.h&#34;\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    delay_init();       //延时函数初始化\n    LED_Init();         //初始化与LED连接的硬件接口\n    while(1)\n    {\n        LED0 = 0;\n        LED1 = 1;\n        delay_ms(300);  //延时300ms\n        LED0 = 1;\n        LED1 = 0;\n        delay_ms(300);  //延时300ms\n    }\n}</code></pre></div><p>是不是看着很舒服，合理缩进、美观、可读性高，是规范的代码风格，当然这只是AStyle一个很基础的功能，其实它支持很多参数，还可以对整个目录及子目录下的源文件进行格式化操作。</p><h2>Keil开发环境添加AStyle插件</h2><p>很多IDE都有自动格式化代码功能，而单片机开发经常使用的Keil系列软件居然没有这个功能，这怎么能忍？还好Keil有自定义插件的功能，可以添加AStyle自动格式化的工具，来格式化我们不规范的代码。</p><h2>1.打开Keil软件</h2><p>选择Tools-&gt;Customize Tools Menu，自定义外部工具菜单。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a53134e5350ed2e4f3f5dc89795f201d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1103\" data-rawheight=\"490\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1103\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a53134e5350ed2e4f3f5dc89795f201d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1103&#39; height=&#39;490&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1103\" data-rawheight=\"490\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1103\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a53134e5350ed2e4f3f5dc89795f201d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a53134e5350ed2e4f3f5dc89795f201d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>2.新建工具</h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a159838903fa9dd9f5a28abce2fc462a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"529\" data-rawheight=\"446\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"529\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a159838903fa9dd9f5a28abce2fc462a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;529&#39; height=&#39;446&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"529\" data-rawheight=\"446\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"529\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a159838903fa9dd9f5a28abce2fc462a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a159838903fa9dd9f5a28abce2fc462a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>点击新建按钮，输入工具名称：<code>Astyle Current File</code>，Command命令选项，指定AStyle.exe的路径，Argument选项输入以下参数，注意大小写，建议复制粘贴，不会出错。</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">-pnUk1s4 --style=ansi !E</code></pre></div><p>这些命令参数的含义，在下面有详细介绍，其中<code>!E</code>表示当前文件，这个参数在Keil软件的使用手册里可以查到。点击OK保存。</p><h2>3.试试格式化效果</h2><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2a294b9f28d32df0ff870e010aa6b17a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"624\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2a294b9f28d32df0ff870e010aa6b17a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;746&#39; height=&#39;624&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"624\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2a294b9f28d32df0ff870e010aa6b17a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2a294b9f28d32df0ff870e010aa6b17a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>好了，现在来试一下一键自动格式化工具吧，无论你的代码写的有多乱，只要点击Tools-&gt;Astyle Current File工具，你就会发现代码一下子变得美观了许多，就像这样。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a7ea4f844b3f1b16ac8710f5d66bdb3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1197\" data-rawheight=\"490\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1197\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a7ea4f844b3f1b16ac8710f5d66bdb3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1197&#39; height=&#39;490&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1197\" data-rawheight=\"490\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1197\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a7ea4f844b3f1b16ac8710f5d66bdb3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7a7ea4f844b3f1b16ac8710f5d66bdb3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>4.定义一个快捷键</h2><p>为了更方便，我们还可以自定义一个快捷键，来执行这个命令。点击工具栏最右边的配置图标，切换到Shortcut Keys选项，选择Tools:Astyle Current File，点击Create Shortcut创建新的快捷键，在弹出的窗口按下你要设置的快捷键，然后保存退出就可以了，下次需要使用的时候，只要按下相对应的快捷键，就可以一键将当前文件格式化。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-65a190c5238fb5502f8baac59e601967_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"886\" data-rawheight=\"789\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"886\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-65a190c5238fb5502f8baac59e601967_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;886&#39; height=&#39;789&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"886\" data-rawheight=\"789\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"886\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-65a190c5238fb5502f8baac59e601967_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-65a190c5238fb5502f8baac59e601967_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>其实，我还是觉得鼠标操作更方便。</b></p><h2>AStyle插件参数详解</h2><p>AStyle插件的参数实在太多了，这里只介绍我们上面那个命令中用到的参数。</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">-pnUk1s4 !E --style=ansi</code></pre></div><p>命令参数详解：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f824fd4723fcdfba1fde4b12e9aa88af_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"649\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f824fd4723fcdfba1fde4b12e9aa88af_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;586&#39; height=&#39;649&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"586\" data-rawheight=\"649\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"586\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f824fd4723fcdfba1fde4b12e9aa88af_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f824fd4723fcdfba1fde4b12e9aa88af_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>更多、更详细的参数说明可以查看自带的帮助文档。</p><h2>BAT命令格式化目录下的源文件</h2><p>下面这个bat命令可以格式化当前目录及子目录下的所有源文件。</p><p>新建bat文件，以记事本打开，输入以下命令：  </p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">for /R %%f in (*.c;*.h) do AStyle.exe --style=allman --indent=spaces=4 --pad-oper --pad-header --unpad-paren --suffix=none --align-pointer=name --lineend=windows --convert-tabs --verbose %%f\npause</code></pre></div><h2>各种代码风格的比较</h2><p>这里只介绍几种常见的代码风格，更多的代码风格参考帮助文档-&gt;Brace Style Options。</p><p><b>allman风格</b></p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Foo(bool isBar)\n{\n    if (isBar)\n    {\n        bar();\n        return 1;\n    }\n    else\n        return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p><b>java风格</b> </p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Foo(bool isBar) {\n    if (isBar) {\n        bar();\n        return 1;\n    } else\n        return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p><b>kr 风格</b></p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Foo(bool isBar)\n{\n    if (isBar) {\n        bar();\n        return 1;\n    } else\n        return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p><b>gnu 风格</b></p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Foo(bool isBar)\n{\n    if (isBar)\n        {\n            bar();\n            return 1;\n        }\n    else\n        return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p><b>linux 风格</b></p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Foo(bool isBar)\n{\n        if (isFoo) {\n                bar();\n                return 1;\n        } else\n                return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><p><b>google 风格</b></p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">int Foo(bool isBar) {\n    if (isBar) {\n        bar();\n        return 1;\n    } else\n        return 0;\n}</code></pre></div><h2>参考资料</h2><ul><li>官方网址：<a "<h2>为什么需要BIN文件呢？</h2><ul><li>有些烧录器只支持BIN文件。</li><li>进行OTA远程升级时，只能使用BIN文件。</li><li>使用JLink脚本文件进行一键烧录时，只支持BIN文件。</li><li>BIN文件要比HEX和AXF文件小的多。</li></ul><p>但Keil默认生成的是AXF和HEX文件格式，那BIN怎么来生成呢？</p><h2>Keil配置生成BIN文件</h2><p>Keil自带了一个小工具，可以通过执行指令来将AXF文件转换为BIN文件这就需要调用一个外部程序fromelf.exe来将AXF文件转换为BIN格式文件。</p><p><code>fromelf.exe</code>文件的位置在安装目录 <code>Keil_v5\\ARM\\ARMCC\\bin</code> 或者 <code>Keil_v5\\ARM\\ARMCC_505u2\\bin</code> 目录下。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e28f2e88d07e65d7fb754afb5904fa7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"756\" data-rawheight=\"284\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"756\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e28f2e88d07e65d7fb754afb5904fa7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;756&#39; height=&#39;284&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"756\" data-rawheight=\"284\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"756\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e28f2e88d07e65d7fb754afb5904fa7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5e28f2e88d07e65d7fb754afb5904fa7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>****在工程配置菜单中，User选项卡，编译后执行的命令，设置为 <code>fromelf --bin -o &#34;$L@L.bin&#34; &#34;#L&#34;</code> ，当然也可以使用上面那种绝对路径的方式，需要看指定fromelf文件的路径，输出BIN文件的路径和生成的AXF文件的路径。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6557067668ba9c737e4d013b83dd074b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"931\" data-rawheight=\"581\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"931\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6557067668ba9c737e4d013b83dd074b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;931&#39; height=&#39;581&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"931\" data-rawheight=\"581\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"931\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6557067668ba9c737e4d013b83dd074b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6557067668ba9c737e4d013b83dd074b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>重新编译，可以看到在输出目录下已经生成了BIN文件。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5b94b3f9623745f1566e2297e20710a4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"761\" data-rawheight=\"318\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"761\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5b94b3f9623745f1566e2297e20710a4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;761&#39; height=&#39;318&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"761\" data-rawheight=\"318\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"761\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5b94b3f9623745f1566e2297e20710a4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5b94b3f9623745f1566e2297e20710a4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><h2>其他开发环境如何将AXF文件转换为BIN文件？</h2><p>当然如果你想把其他开发环境生成的AXF文件转换为BIN文件，也可以直接调用这个小工具来实现。</p><h2>命令格式为：</h2><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">[fromelf.exe文件路径] --bin -o [BIN路径} [AXF文件路径}</code></pre></div><p>如：</p><div class=\"highlight\"><pre><code class=\"language-text\">E:/Keil_v5/ARM/ARMCC/bin/fromelf.exe --bin -o E:/Keil_Project/OneNET.bin E:/Keil_Project/OneNET.axf</code></pre></div><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-24b9d37753820d9311bf65bd171707d8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1357\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1357\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-24b9d37753820d9311bf65bd171707d8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1357&#39; height=&#39;395&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1357\" data-rawheight=\"395\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\"             "title": "我的互联网产品观", 
            "content": "<p>新开通了个公众号，准备认真的记录自己的职业、生活、情感和人生体验。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这个公众号，是准备用日记的方式来记录的，给别人看，更多的是给自己看的，写的东西应该会都比较接地气，也欢迎大家订阅关注，并能够留言讨论。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-070bcb17a618cb4bcc743df16737398e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"689\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-070bcb17a618cb4bcc743df16737398e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;689&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"689\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-070bcb17a618cb4bcc743df16737398e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-070bcb17a618cb4bcc743df16737398e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u><b>公众号第一篇写什么？</b></u></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>想来想去，觉得还是从工作开始写吧。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>熟悉我的人都知道，过往我一直在TMT行业工作，也一直在做互联网相关的工作，研发、产品、营销、销售、业务全部都做过，因此，这一篇既是这个公众号的开篇，又是对过往工作的一个总结。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9c5d7cec3c7cb4a0c1e0c7d30a2b3d70_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"856\" data-rawheight=\"458\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"856\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9c5d7cec3c7cb4a0c1e0c7d30a2b3d70_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;856&#39; height=&#39;458&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"856\" data-rawheight=\"458\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"856\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9c5d7cec3c7cb4a0c1e0c7d30a2b3d70_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9c5d7cec3c7cb4a0c1e0c7d30a2b3d70_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b><u>谈谈我的互联网产品观</u></b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>下面列出的都是我自己的观点，一定不全正确，也一定是片面的，期待大家指正哦。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>我们国家的互联网企业，绝大部分从本质上解决的还是连接的问题。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>核心是把现存的闲置/冗余/割裂的资源，做个连接和整合罢了，<u><b>实际上是资源再分配的过程，并不是真正的资源新创造</b></u>，更多的还是在生产关系上做改良和优化，底层的生产力没有实质的提升。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>这种模式，当然也有意义。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>在资源整合没有到上限的时候，可以享受到资源红利。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>但一旦资源整合到达上限，资源红利消失，就会变成残酷无效的零和博弈，某一方利益增加，必然会有另一方利益收缩。所谓的“羊毛出在猪身上”，不外如此，这也是为啥互联网公司喜欢补贴、喜欢将对手赶尽杀绝的根本原因。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>我认为互联网最大的优势就是“边际成本递减”的技术优势，固定的成本结构下，用户越多，单用户成本越低，再通过增值服务获取利润，所以广告、游戏容易出利润。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而对于O2O、电商等互联网平台，它们的利润不会那么明显的原因是，针对每个用户的服务，其中涉及到的短距物流或快递费用是无法边际递减的，每个用户享受服务时都是需要刚性的额外支出这个成本，所以利润不容易大规模出现。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>而上面所述的问题，也是为什么大的电商平台必定要整合优化物流平台的原因，比如京东物流和菜鸟物流，他们想做的其实还是通过并单配送、分点建仓等技术手段来实现对单人线下服务的边际成本递减。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u><b>互联网模式无非如此，核心在于“边际成本递减”、“大数原理”、“开放共享”等技术基础。</b></u></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u><b>我关于“用户体验”的理解</b></u><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>提到互联网，必定提到“用户体验”，甚至很多人都会第一优先提到“用户体验”。包括一些业外人士，他们对于互联网的理解，可能更多的都是被业内人士传播的“用户体验”，好像“用户体验”就是互联网产品的全部了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>我觉得这是非常不对的，<u><b>互联网跟任何行业都没有区别，第一优先要解决的是某些用户在某些场景下的某些问题</b></u>，是解决现存需求的，在解决了现存需求的情况下才有后续所谓的“用户体验”。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>还是周鸿祎在他最新那本书里面说的对，互联网产品核心就是三个要素：<u><b>“刚需、痛点、高频”</b></u>，他说的真的对，真的不是啥“用户体验”，请问去医院排队看医生的体验很好么？但生病了还不是得去嘛？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>就因为所谓的“用户体验”，导致太多平庸的产品经理们，在一堆不知道因为什么原因而存在的伪需求的互联网产品里，浪费青春，天天在纠结这个按钮放这里还是那里，这个要用线还是空白，真的是浪费时间的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><u><b>产品的核心真的不是用户体验，而是业务模型，而是“刚需、痛点、高频”。</b></u></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>我还看到，有些所谓智能硬件的互联网产品，让人觉得莫名其妙，比如：</p><p>用个手机App操作你家里的电饭煲做饭，这个很搞笑，电饭煲要想工作不还是得自己首先淘米、洗米、放米嘛，你说手机App就弄个开关，有什么用呢？那还不如用普通电饭煲都有的定时功能呢。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>总结下，<u><b>互联网跟任何行业都没有区别，第一优先要解决的是某些用户在某些场景下的某些问题</b></u>，核心三要素，<u><b>刚需、痛点、高频</b></u>！！！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>微信：neutyz，公众号：U-4EverYoung，关注交流！</p><p></p>",

            "content": "<p> 小编这篇给大家带来的是如何用opencv在视野中识别出A4纸或者是某一个具体的靶标什么的，同样的算法改改可以用来识别其他的形状的物体，先来看看实际的效果：</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1860e0c20e3fefeade8f4c9b2ff88d77_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"185\" data-rawheight=\"268\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"185\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;174&#39; height=&#39;266&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"174\" data-rawheight=\"266\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"174\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e9c13f81940b31681b8afb1d9f98d0d0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>由于小编是在虚拟机下调用摄像头出现了一些问题，还没有试试连续过程中的识别情况，等摄像头到了，小编会再后续中测试。</p><p>在程序开始之前我们先梳理一下解决这个问题的流程：</p><p>1、图像预处理（这里考虑到处理速度问题采用的是高斯滤波）</p><p>2、边缘检测（本文采用的canny算子）</p><p>3、膨胀（尽量使边缘闭合）</p><p>4、寻找A4边框（采用的是findContours算法）</p><p>5、对findContours识别出来的轮廓进行排除得到我们需要的轮廓，这是最为核心的一步。譬如本文是筛选类似A4纸书本这样的框，采用的方法是先对得到的轮廓进行凸包拟合，然后以四边形和每个夹角大于60作为这样的一个初步筛选。然后从筛选出来的轮廓中选择最大的那个就是我们想要的了。（注：由于本文是一个demo，筛选条件比较简单，读者结合自己的应用常见和识别对象可以利用譬如直方图统计这样的增加筛选成功率）</p><p>6、得到满足筛选条件的最大轮廓的四个顶点（方便后面做透视校正，小编会在后面陆续写出分享）</p><p>7、绘出我们的轮廓</p><p>下面给出具体代码，有以问的欢迎留言交流：</p><p>#include &lt;QCoreApplication&gt;</p><p>#include &lt;opencv2/core/core.hpp&gt;</p><p>#include &lt;opencv2/highgui/highgui.hpp&gt;</p><p>#include &lt;opencv2/imgproc/imgproc.hpp&gt; //图像处理头文件</p><p>#include &lt;cv.h&gt;</p><p>#include &lt;highgui.h&gt;</p><p>#include &lt;iostream&gt;</p><p>using namespace cv;</p><p>using namespace std;</p><p>//根据三个点计算中间那个点的夹角，这里是用三角变换，感兴趣的可以求一下公式的推导   pt1 pt0 pt2</p><p>double getAngle(cv::Point pt1, cv::Point pt2, cv::Point pt0)</p><p>{</p><p>    double dx1 = pt1.x - pt0.x;</p><p>    double dy1 = pt1.y - pt0.y;</p><p>    double dx2 = pt2.x - pt0.x;</p><p>    double dy2 = pt2.y - pt0.y;</p><p>    return (dx1*dx2 + dy1*dy2)/sqrt((dx1*dx1 + dy1*dy1)*(dx2*dx2 + dy2*dy2) + 1e-10);</p><p>}</p><p>//寻找最大边框</p><p>int findLargestSquare(const vector&lt;vector&lt;cv::Point&gt; &gt;&amp; squares, vector&lt;cv::Point&gt;&amp; biggest_square)</p><p>{</p><p>    if (!squares.size()) return -1;</p><p>    int max_width = 0;</p><p>    int max_height = 0;</p><p>    int max_square_idx = 0;</p><p>    for (int i = 0; i &lt; squares.size(); i++)</p><p>    {</p><p>        cv::Rect rectangle = boundingRect(Mat(squares[i]));</p><p>        if ((rectangle.width &gt;= max_width) &amp;&amp; (rectangle.height &gt;= max_height))</p><p>        {</p><p>            max_width = rectangle.width;</p><p>            max_height = rectangle.height;</p><p>            max_square_idx = i;</p><p>        }</p><p>    }</p><p>    biggest_square = squares[max_square_idx];</p><p>    return max_square_idx;</p><p>}</p><p>//主函数，小编这里反省一下，没有把一些函数封装起来，显得比较乱，小编建议大家养成把处理得函数都封装起来，主函数就不会像小编这样看上去很乱了。</p><p>int main(int argc, char *argv[])</p><p>{</p><p>    Mat src,dst,gray,binarization,open,dilate_img,gauss_img,edges_img;</p><p>   src = imread(&#34;/home/shangbinbin/opencv_linux_test/test3/4.jpg&#34;);</p><p>//处理为灰度图</p><p>  cvtColor(src,gray,CV_BGR2GRAY);</p><p>//高斯滤波</p><p>  GaussianBlur(gray,gauss_img,Size(3,3),2,2);</p><p>//边缘检测</p><p>  Canny(gauss_img,edges_img,50,150,3);</p><p>//膨胀</p><p>  dilate(edges_img, dilate_img, Mat(), cv::Point(-1, -1), 3, 1, 1);</p><p>//定义容器类型得变量，不太明白得可以看看C++的容器这一部分知识</p><p>  vector&lt;vector&lt;cv::Point&gt; &gt; contours, squares, hulls;</p><p>  //寻找出所有闭合的边框</p><p>  findContours(dilate_img, contours, RETR_LIST, CHAIN_APPROX_SIMPLE);</p><p>  vector&lt;cv::Point&gt; hull, approx;</p><p>//筛选边框</p><p>   for (int i = 0; i &lt; contours.size(); i++)</p><p>   {</p><p>       //获得轮廓的凸包</p><p>       convexHull(contours[i], hull);</p><p>       //多边形拟合凸包边框(此时的拟合的精度较低)</p><p>       //arcLength得到轮廓的长度</p><p>      approxPolyDP(Mat(hull), approx, arcLength(Mat(hull), true)*0.02, true);</p><p>      //筛选出四边形的各个角度都接近直角的凸四边形</p><p>              if (approx.size() ==4 &amp;&amp; isContourConvex(Mat(approx))&amp;&amp; fabs(contourArea(Mat(approx))) &lt; 1166400)</p><p>              {</p><p>                  double maxCosine = 0;</p><p>                  for (int j = 2; j &lt; 5; j++)</p><p>                  {</p><p>                      double cosine = fabs(getAngle(approx[j%4], approx[j-2], approx[j-1]));</p><p>                      maxCosine = MAX(maxCosine, cosine);</p><p>                  }</p><p>                      //角度大概72度</p><p>                  if (maxCosine &lt; 0.4)</p><p>                  {</p><p>                      squares.push_back(approx);</p><p>                      hulls.push_back(hull);</p><p>                   }</p><p>               }</p><p>   }</p><p>   vector&lt;cv::Point&gt; largest_square;</p><p>   //找出外接矩形最大的四边形</p><p>   int idex = findLargestSquare(squares, largest_square);</p><p> //画图</p><p>   for (int i = 0; i &lt; 4; i++)</p><p>   {</p><p>                // circle(src,squares[idex][i],5,Scalar(0,0,255), 5);</p><p>       if(i&lt;3)</p><p>       {</p><p>               line(src, squares[idex][i], squares[idex][i+1], Scalar(0,0,255), 5);</p><p>       }</p><p>       else</p><p>           line(src, squares[idex][3], squares[idex][0], Scalar(0,0,255), 5);</p><p>   }</p><p> //显示出来</p><p>   namedWindow(&#34;draw&#34;, CV_WINDOW_NORMAL);</p><p>   imshow(&#34;draw&#34;,src);</p><p>   waitKey(0);</p><p>   return 0;</p><p>}</p>",

            "content": "<p>自从写了上一篇文章以后，咨询我工作的突然变多了，虽然大部分情况下我也不知道这个公司到底怎么样。甚至有研一的问实习什么的之类的问题，觉得有必要趁着写论文浮躁不如再写一篇文章介绍我找实习的历程。</p><p>一共拿了五个实习offer——SK海力士、博世—BSH、和舰科技、春秋航空、舍弗勒。最终去了博西华和SK海力士。</p><p><b>1.SK海力士</b></p><p>5.12去东南大学的实习双选会，东大应该是南京的第一场。排着队投了简历，下午十二点多收到面试通知，等着面试。六个人群面，两位面试官。没问专业什么的问题。先做自我介绍，然后问打算在半导体行业呆多久，然后就是每人不同的个性化的问题。</p><p>面试完以后通过了面试。后面需要做一个性格测试，非常难做，12秒内完成一题，一共好像需要做400道题，据说在韩国批改。</p><p>然后就是实习，实习在八月份，一共两周，在BSH请了两周假。实习前三天就是听课两天半，最后半天参观环境安全馆。听课还要笔试，很幸运地听人事说我是笔试第一名。第四天素质拓展，然后去部门实习，我去了ETCH。部门内人非常好，还参观了世界上最干净的无尘车间，技术真厉害。</p><p>最后就是个人陈述和集体陈述。就是在个人陈述的时候被告知笔试第一，挺惊讶的。然后结营，后面体检发offer什么的都是后话了。</p><p>非常喜欢这家公司，在实习的时候也非常深入的了解了这家公司。免费班车，免费宿舍，免费食堂。最大的收获就是深入地了解了这家公司吧。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-215e0e5360d168a4af8c036e49784083_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1440\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-215e0e5360d168a4af8c036e49784083_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1440&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1440\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-215e0e5360d168a4af8c036e49784083_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-215e0e5360d168a4af8c036e49784083_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>2.博世——BSH</b></p><p>实习僧投递的简历，没多久人事邀约面试，直接用人部门面试，实习生不用人事面。第一次面试是为北航毕业的前辈，问我了不了解洗衣机结构，磕磕巴巴说不出来，还介绍了工作内容，问了口语，那时候口语比较差。说起口语，感谢博西家电的实习让我口语已经达到了能和德国工程师人一起做实验和技术交流的程度，对我收获很大。</p><p>BSH的第一次面试很差，感觉没戏了，人事又来了电话说有个岗位更适合我，介绍了岗位的主要工作内容，于是在去面试这个部门。这次由于提前作了准备，而且问我最多的都是我的课题，所以我还是比较面的成功的。面试结束后人事说好好干，你的岗位干的好了可以留用......</p><p>然后体检，2018.6.6日正式入职世界百强企业博世集团，公司还给办了招行金卡。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c862f096d6f3e816ea151ea7b6096e2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1440\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c862f096d6f3e816ea151ea7b6096e2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1440&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1440\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c862f096d6f3e816ea151ea7b6096e2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4c862f096d6f3e816ea151ea7b6096e2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>主要工作内容就是研发与测试，包括整机测试、零部件测试。很有挑战性的工作，实习了四个多月。反正在这里工作不是螺丝钉，更能发挥个人价值吧。</p><p>虽然只是实习生，可这里的同事都把我当做是正式员工，这一点我很欣慰。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>3.和舰科技</b></p><p>苏州一家著名的半导体公司，看辅导员群里发的消息，实习一周，投了简历可能觉得我简历比较漂亮于是没有面试直接录用......</p><p>当时在BSH实习，想着后面海力士实习还要两周于是就没请假，放弃了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>4.春秋航空</b></p><p>5.26日在南京理工大学面的春秋航空，人事很吃惊，说每次去你们南航都没几个人，今天在南理工怎么还有主动送上门来的。然后面试，岗位是机务，人事说我比较优秀说毕业给我转管培生的职位。问的问题就是对机务的了解之类的，还问了杂七杂八毕业时间等等。</p><p>后面也没去，他给我打了好几个电话让我慎重考虑，还说你是航空院校的，去博世做什么家电多不对口啊，航空院校就应该来航空公司嘛。毕竟机务太辛苦，春秋航空机务不如劳斯莱斯的机务挣得多，算了。至于管培生，我还是觉得外资企业的管培生更有含金量。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>5.舍弗勒</b></p><p>最后一个实习offer，当时也纠结去BSH还是同为德企的舍弗勒。</p><p>舍弗勒在南京理工宣讲会我没去也没网申，然后第二天正好就是南理工大型双选会，他正好安排面试，我就去霸面了，霸面以后他对我感觉不错，让我回去完善资料，做好网申。</p><p>然后过了几天没消息我以为凉了，结果没多久又让我去南航面试，我回复短信在南理工面过了还需要来不，回复最好来吧。然后通过，足足问了我40分钟，和我同去的20分钟就结束了......</p><p>考虑到舍弗勒实习日期短，海力士不好请假就没去，后面才知道还可以续日期，而且舍弗勒实习工资超高，是我在BSH的两倍。</p><p>对了，面的南京的舍弗勒，不是太仓的，太仓的还要过去租房子。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>舍弗勒英文面试问我的问题</b></p><p>1.你的爱好是什么，为什么你喜欢它</p><p>2.当你压力大的时候你会做什么</p><p>3.在一个团队中你喜欢担任什么样的职位，为什么？</p><p><b>舍弗勒笔试（选择题）</b></p><p><i>1.</i></p><p><i>You are in a project meeting where your immediate manager and the Department Head are discussing a certain aspect of the project. The situation and problems are complex and certain areas are even beyond your understanding but it looks like there are only 2 possible options at this point in time. It becomes clear to you that the two of them have very different and strong opinions about which decision and direction should be appropriate to take. Each has his own views, with a good mix of strong arguments for his decision, with identified limitations, risks and potential consequences. They have turned to you to ask you for your opinion and to choose which one you will support. What do you do?</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. Since both options have their own share of benefits and risk and limitations, it makes more sense for me to support my immediate manager since he will have more influence over my daily work and year-end appraisal. </i></p><p><i>B. The Department Head is obviously more senior in rank and experienced in such matters. It is also more appropriate to support him as he is the overall person in charge and will make the final decision anyway. </i></p><p><i>C.This is an awkward situation. They may have personal differences that I am not aware of and it is best for me not to take sides and get involved. I will declare that I am new and inexperienced and will defer to any decision made as I am sure it will be the best. </i></p><p><i>D. I consider all points of discussion, combine the best of both options and offer this as a better alternative which would be ideal for the situation. </i></p><p><i>E. I consider both options carefully and select one of them, with my own comments and reasons.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>2.</i></p><p><i>You work in a team of 5 with a supervisor and a manager managing your team and other teams in this department. In your first project within your team, in one of the internal discussions, you feel that some figures are interpreted and presented inaccurately although the primary data and facts are accurate. You raised your questions and concerns to the team leader, David. David is one of your co-workers who is the most senior in terms of years of service. He appears to have good relationships with everyone, especially with the supervisor. David listens to you but feels confident about the situation and thinks that the interpretation is not inaccurate and even if it is, the primary data and facts remain unchanged and are easily accessible by most people involved in the project. This is a team project and one of many that you will be involved in, mostly with members of your same team. What do you do?</i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABCDE</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. I will just let the situation remain as it is since I have done my part in raising my concerns and questions and received his response. Afterall, David will be responsible for the project and should be able to respond to any questions asked. </i></p><p><i>B. Since David does not want to listen to me and make any changes, I feel that I will need to speak to my Department Head about this. It will be more appropriate for the Department Head to address this sensitive situation than for me to push on. </i></p><p><i>C. I raise my concern immediately with our supervisor and voiced my displeasure about how uncooperative David has been and how he appears so unconcerned about the quality of the data used and how this may affect the project&#39;s success. </i></p><p><i>D. I discussed with other team members to cross check my understanding of the situation and whether my assumptions and thinking are also shared. If there is a common understanding of the situation, I will again try to confront David, perhaps with other team members, to clarify the situation. </i></p><p><i>E. I call to arrange a meeting with David and our supervisor to confront the issue as I feel that it is important to clarify the situation and problem once and for all.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>3.</i></p><p><i>You are currently researching some material to support your team leader on a project involving the development of a new process. The project is of high importance and is closely watched by the CEO due to the potential benefits it could bring to the company. The deadline for submitting your research material is by tomorrow morning, the deadline cannot be delayed as it will affect other stages of the project. At noon, your supervisor asked you to read a set of presentation material which is required for tomorrow&#39;s breakfast meeting with some customers. Your role tomorrow will be to meet, greet and brief the customers and you will be supporting a discussion session. You have supported a similar event last year and played a similar role as well. However, you know that the research still requires more time and it is likely you may need your evening time as well to complete the task. What do you do? </i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABCDE</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. The research work is clearly more important. I will explain my situation to my supervisor and politely request to be excused from the breakfast meeting as I am sure he will understand. </i></p><p><i>B. I will read the presentation material early tomorrow morning and continue with my research in order to complete my current task. </i></p><p><i>C. I will read the presentation material straight away and check with my supervisor for any guidance and confirm my role for tomorrow&#39;s breakfast meeting. Then, I will continue my research work. </i></p><p><i>D. I will continue my research and quickly complete and submit this somehow by 5pm. Then, I can read the presentation material for the breakfast meeting and complete this before I go off for the day. </i></p><p><i>E. I will place my research as a priority and only read the presentation material if I have time. I am confident of managing through the situation tomorrow morning as I am familiar with the event.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>4.</i></p><p><i>You have been asked to participate in a cross-functional team to work on a certain topical problem which is not your familiar area of knowledge. At the same time, you are asked to work on another project in your department. This project topic is more familiar as you have handled a similar project previously. You have complete freedom to choose either project, but you can only choose one. What do you do? </i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--AB</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. I will choose the project in the cross functional team and try my best and hope that I can be of help and learn as much as I can at the same time. </i></p><p><i>B. I feel that choosing a project not in my familiar area is risky and also will limit the contributions to the company in that project. I will therefore stick to the project in my department as I feel I can contribute more quickly and greatly to this area. This will also allow me to return to my regular role quickly.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>5.</i></p><p><i>You have just been promoted to handle a new small team whom you have not worked with before. You are aware that there are performance issues for a long time. Many of the team members are long-time staff in the company although not all have been in the same team together for that long. Your manager has asked you to fix the situation quickly because this is exactly you why you have been promoted. What is your preferred way of dealing with this situation?</i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABC</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. I quickly announced to the team that I have taken over as their leader, declare that poor performance issues will not be tolerated anymore and ask everyone to raise his/her level of performance from this day onwards. </i></p><p><i>B. I try to make friends with as many members of the team as possible and persuade them to improve their performance over time. It is more practical this way as this will ensure that I can manage the motivation level, retain everyone in the team and ensure a more sustainable improvement over time. </i></p><p><i>C. I take some time to understand the performance issues and process, in addition, I will get insight and feedback from people working within and outside the team. I then communicate to the team the situation and impact of the problems to other teams and the company. I share my plans and try to create an open environment where my team members can approach me with any questions.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>6.</i></p><p><i>You are writing a report to submit to your immediate manager for a project. A more experienced member of the team informs you that she thinks the report could be improved if you change the order and content of certain sections. What do you do?</i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABCD</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. I quickly make the changes she suggested and thank her for being helpful. </i></p><p><i>B. I thank her for her comments and suggestions but decide that it is wiser to stick to my original work so that I can be proud of it. Even if I am not perfect, the work is truly mine and not helped by anyone. </i></p><p><i>C. I make selective changes to the report only where it matters. </i></p><p><i>D. I discuss with her to understand her reasons for the changes proposed before deciding whether and how much to change the report.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>7.</i></p><p><i>You are about to start your rotation in the Finance department as part of the training for new graduates. You will be joining the Finance department at the busiest period of the year when it is involved in annual business and budget planning. Your new supervisor briefly informed you 2 weeks before you are due to go over that you will be joining a special project team in Finance to support the development of a new process and tool supporting budget planning. You have not worked in any Finance role before. What do you do?</i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABCD</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. I research the internet to find out everything about business planning an annual budgeting process. </i></p><p><i>B. I will speak to my current supervisor to request for early release and transfer to the Finance department so that I can have a headstart to the project and get to meet my new colleagues. </i></p><p><i>C. Thank the new supervisor and request her to email you more information about the project so that you can be more prepared. </i></p><p><i>D. Thank the new supervisor and inform her that you would like to meet up with her next week to find out more about the details of the project you will be involved in.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>8.</i></p><p><i>You have arranged to meet up with a colleague from another department in order to explain about the project you are leading and request for the information you need. Your colleague arrived on time and mention that she could only spare half an hour instead of one hour. During the meeting, your colleague appears distracted and in a rush. She apologised and hands you some pieces of paper stating that the information contained should be enough for you to get started. After the meeting, you reviewed the information thoroughly and feel that you do not have everything that you need for your project. What do you do?</i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABCD</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. Call my colleague to clarify the information she provided and the need for more data. Get started with the areas of information I feel more confident about. </i></p><p><i>B. I know my colleague is busy and I will stick to the information given and make the best out of it. </i></p><p><i>C. Send an email to the colleague with all the questions I want the answers to. </i></p><p><i>D. Wait till my colleague has more time to spare before I approach her on the same topic.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>9.</i></p><p><i>You accompanied your Sales Manager to the site of Customer A to support a customer survey exercise. The survey interview is held in a meeting room. Just as you are about to complete your interview with Customer A, you received a call on silent mode, and you recognize that it is from Customer C. You guess that Customer C may want to discuss some things concerning the same survey you had earlier conducted as he had some questions the last time. What do you do next? </i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABCD</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. Ask my Sales Manager to help me continue and conclude the survey so that I can take the call from Customer C immediately. </i></p><p><i>B. Excuse myself from the meeting room immediately to take the call from Customer C. </i></p><p><i>C. Pick up the call and inform Customer C that I would call him/her back later as I was in the middle of another meeting. </i></p><p><i>D. Do not pick up the call. Call Customer C back later.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>10.</i></p><p><i>You have just received a brief email from another manager, highlighting that you could have been more tactful and diplomatic in your response to a customer&#39;s challenge on some quality issues. What do you do? </i></p><p><i>--请选择--</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>--请选择--ABCD</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><i>A. Reply to the other manager, thank him and explain politely and factually what happened and why I maintain that it was appropriate for me to do so. </i></p><p><i>B. Decide not to make an issue of it and let the email go unreplied since my immediate manager did not comment me on the same thing. </i></p><p><i>C. Call the other manager up immediately to find out more about his point of view. </i></p><p><i>D. Check with my immediate manager to get his feedback on the same situation before reaching out to the other manager to understand his comments.</i></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>总的来说，还是非常感谢这两段实习经历，这也是我能获得14个offer的必要条件之一吧。就算没时间实习，导师不放人，也可以去面试一下实习，提高自己的面试能力，省的等秋招到了有点措不及手。</p><p></p>",
